# Yet Another Mech Variants List

The following list contains a total of 2,819 'mech variants from Mechwarrior 5 with Yet Another Mechlab using the following additional mods:
* Exotic IS Mechs (by IR0NPENGUIN)
* Wasp YAML-Edition (by Mace24de / Zombeh)
* YA Shade Mech (by LtShade, TePa)
* YAGDM (by EmpressDaystar)
* Yet Another Campaign Hero Mech (by [DeadRaiser](https://www.nexusmods.com/users/41300230))
* Yet Another Faction Variant (by Tender Tendrils)
* Yet Another IS Mech (by [DeadRaiser](https://www.nexusmods.com/users/41300230))
* Yet Another Legendary Mech (by Malum Umbra)
* Yet Another Mechlab (by [cszolee79 and trueg](https://www.nexusmods.com/mechwarrior5mercenaries/mods/459))
* Yet Another Mechlab Mechs Maintenance Fork (by Chozo4. Forked by phfor)
* Yet Another Special Variant (by trueg)
* YetAnotherClanMech (by cszolee79 and trueg)
## Light Mechs
